<Rate>5< /Rate><Review>Hidden gem! Sophia's is set back from the Paradise main drag, Skyway, just enough that you could easily drive right by and never notice it. That would be HUGE mistake! Everyone in our five person group had something different and we all loved our dishes.

I love yellow curry and struggle to find places that make it the way I enjoy. The yellow curry with tofu was PHENOMENAL! It was just right in the heat department and off the charts in the flavor department. Even the steamed rice was flavorful by itself. I never knew rice could taste so good.

My wife enjoyed the fried rice with tofu. She said it was one of her favorite fried rice dishes. Good flavor and not oily. She would definitely come back.

Service was prompt; we were there at lunchtime during the work week. The gentleman who served us was nice and polite.

My only negative is this place isn't close to my home that is 8 hours away. Whenever we are back in Paradise or Chico, we will be stopping in! You should do the same.< /Review><Pics>None<//Pics>< resp>

<Text>I generally approve of this place, but there was one aspect about it I absolutely needed to comment on:

I honestly can't tell if maybe it's just a different preparation style, but I suspect they hold onto the tofu for too long. It tastes sour the same way mine does when it starts to get close to the expiration date. I'm hesitant to complain because I personally haven't yet gotten sick from it and I in fact like the slightly pungent flavor, but because it seems most likely this is an accident, I still thought someone should tell them to keep a better eye on their ingredients before a customer is made ill.

PS, a lot of people on here are complaining about the service, and even as someone who likes this place I'll say that's a fair criticism. It's one of those "everyone's doing their best" small businesses where they're understaffed but very friendly and engaging. Again, I do recommend the restaurant... provided you don't have somewhere you need to be.</Text>< pictures>

Israel (the owner is very hands-on on the business and is customer focused. < Text>
Decent place to eat if you don't want to wait.  We have been many times and will probably be back.  It's not spectacular, but not horrible (hence the 3 stars).  They do like to use "Chef Mic" (microwave) often, but other than that seems okay.  We have been for the Sunday brunch and were not really impressed.  They have a lot of food, but it's all pretty forgettable.  The omelette, pancake, waffle station where they will make options on demand was pretty good and definitely fresh compared to the rest of the food.  The pie table was pretty good and a good deal as a pie there is pretty expensive.  So...go get and omelette and some pie and be happy.  They are not that busy, so I'm not sure how much longer they will be in business there...however, they have been there for some time and have survived, so who knows.  We will continue to go there as long as they are there.< /Text>

<user_name>Sandra Lyons< /user_name><Text>Friendly staff, good food at mostly reasonable prices. Having been away for several years and now back here in our favorite area it was great to revisit Marie's. The decor has not changed, we noticed most of the food items are still available. <review>To be clear, this review is solely based on my experiences ordering and picking up pies for Thanksgiving and Christmas this year.  I ordered three MC pies a few days before Thanksgiving.  I did not sit on hold for too long and the customer service was very professional and courteous.  When I arrived the day before Thanksgiving to pick them up, the parking lot was absolute chaos!  I had to park over by Michael's!  I was highly impressed to be greeted by a host at the front door and directed where to go upon my arrival.  The pickup routine was organized very well (prepaid pies go through one direction/entrance and unpaid, pre-orders through another).  Just for the pie pickups alone, it was very well staffed with clusters of employees finding the order, another retrieving your pies, and another responsible for check-out.  I actually added my Banana Cream to my order and it was no problem.  I was in and out of there in minutes, the customer service was friendly and warm, there is a board kept updated and within a central view to see what pies are available in stock if you want to add to your order.  Not to mention, all of the sides they had prepared and wrapped and priced as well!  Very smooth, very easy, in and out!  Christmas Eve was much less crowded.  I pre-ordered online which was very convenient and even if I had lost my confirmation email, they have their own copy when you check in.  I hope to find time to go in and enjoy a meal there one of these days!  Also, their pies are outstanding!  We've had pumpkin, lemon meringue, banana cream, and lemon dream...They are all fantastic!<//review>< username>

<user>110704425369812342044< /user><name>Jennifer Chesley< /name>< Time>
1545961488153</Time>
<rating>4<//rating>< Review>
To be clear, this review is solely based on my experiences ordering and picking up pies for Thanksgiving and Christmas this year.  I ordered three MC pies a few days before Thanksgiving.  I did not sit on hold for too long and the customer service was very professional and courteous.  When I arrived the day before Thanksgiving to pick them up, the parking lot was absolute chaos!  I had to park over by Michael's!  I was highly impressed to be greeted by a host at the front door and directed where to go upon my arrival.  The pickup routine was organized very well (prepaid pies go through one direction/entrance and unpaid, pre-orders through another).  Just for the pie pickups alone, it was very well staffed with clusters of employees finding the order, another retrieving your pies, and another responsible for check-out.  I actually added my Banana Cream to my order and it was no problem.  I was in and out of there in minutes, the customer service was friendly and warm, there is a board kept updated and within a central view to see what pies are available in stock if you want to add to your order.  Not to mention, all of the sides they had prepared and wrapped and priced as well!  Very smooth, very easy, in and out!  Christmas Eve was much less crowded.  I pre-ordered online which was very convenient and even if I had lost my confirmation email, they have their own copy when you check in.  I hope to find time to go in and enjoy a meal there one of these days!  Also, their pies are outstanding!  We've had pumpkin, lemon meringue, banana cream, and lemon dream...They are all fantastic!</Review>

So I asked our server to have it turned down. She returned after about 2 mins, and said no. So I went to talk with the manager. He was a jerk! He said that they would not turn it down because someone just came into the bar area and wanted it that loud. The volume was so overbearing that it ruined our meal. I said this to the manager, who again refused to turn it down, so I said that we wanted half of the cost deducted from my wife's meal because she could no longer continue eating. He gave off a very rude smirk with sigh of disgust, so I asked that he not do that. He immediately argued that he wasn't smirking, so I asked: "What? Do I have to take a photo and show you?" He replied, and I'm not exaggerating: "If you take a photo of me, I'll sue you!" Then he immediately left and went directly into the kitchen. I took photos of our bill and payment for proof, then informed the police. Needless to say, we will NEVER go back there.</Text>

<Date>1243528072449<//Date>< review>
We ordered some take-out dinners from Marie Callender's recently - turkey dinner, pot pie, and two kids dinners.  The presentation was pretty bad - pie was smashed, kids dinners just rolling around, potatoes/stuffing clearly served with an ice cream scoop - although some of that may be because it was take out.  None of the dinners were anything to write home about taste-wise, either.  The menu hypes the pot pie, so we were disappointed it wasn't better.

The dessert pies were better, but again not as good as one might think given how much they focus on them.  Although the regular apple pie was a little bland, the french apple was better, and the lemon meringue was good.  The kids scarfed down the chocolate pie.<//review>
